       $(function(){
 			$('#slides').slides({
 				preload: true,
 				preloadImage: 'http://www.ldap.cz/img/loading.gif',
 				currentClass: 'crent',
 				play: 7000,
 				pause: 7000,
 				hoverPause: true,
 				animationStart: function(current){
 					$('.caption').animate({
 						bottom:-35
 					},100);
 					if (window.console && console.log) {
 						// example return of current slide number
 						console.log('animationStart on slide: ', current);
 					};
 				},
 				animationComplete: function(current){
 					$('.caption').animate({
 						bottom:0
 					},200);
 					if (window.console && console.log) {
 						// example return of current slide number
 						console.log('animationComplete on slide: ', current);
 					};
 				},
 				slidesLoaded: function() {
 					$('.caption').animate({
 						bottom:0
 					},200);
 				}
 			});
 		});
      </script>

      <script>
       function turnToPage(page, maxpage, slide)
 {
 	currentPage = page;
   resetPaging(maxpage)
 	$('.strankovac').removeClass('active');
 	$('.strankovac'+currentPage).addClass('active');
 	$('.strana').hide();
 	$('.stranaR'+currentPage).show();
 	
 	/*if(slide == true)
 	{
 	$('html, body').animate({
     scrollTop: 100
 		 }, 500);
 	}*/
 }
 
 function resetPaging(maxpage)
 {
 	$('.doleva').css('visibility','visible');
 	$('.doleva').unbind('click');
 	$('.doprava').css('visibility','visible');
 	$('.doprava').unbind('click');
 	
 	
 	if(currentPage == 1)
 	{
 	 	$('.doleva').css('visibility','hidden');
 	}
 	if(currentPage == maxpage)
 	{
 	 	$('.doprava').css('visibility','hidden');	 	
 	}
 	$('.strankovani .active').removeClass('active');
 	
 	$('.doleva').bind('click',function(){
 	 turnToPage(currentPage-1, maxpage, false);
 	});
 	$('.doprava').bind('click',function(){
 	 turnToPage(currentPage+shownPages, maxpage, false);
 	});
 }
 
 	var currentPage = 1;
 	var maxpage = 59;
 	var shownPages = 1;
 	turnToPage(1, maxpage, false);
 
 	function upravitOdkazy(that)
 	{
 		var hodnota = that.parent().find('input').val();
 		var novaHodnota = Math.ceil(hodnota / that.parent().find('input').attr('rel')) * that.parent().find('input').attr('rel');
 		that.parent().find('a').attr('href',root+'koupit/'+that.parent().find('a').attr('rel')+'/'+novaHodnota+'/');
 	}
 	function prepocitatNaMOQ(that)
 	{
 		var hodnota = that.parent().find('input').val();
 		var novaHodnota = Math.ceil(hodnota / that.parent().find('input').attr('rel')) * that.parent().find('input').attr('rel');
 		that.parent().find('input').val(novaHodnota);
 	}
 
 	$(function(){
 		$('.amount').focusout(function(){
 			prepocitatNaMOQ($(this));
 			upravitOdkazy($(this));
 		});
 		
 		$('.amount').keyup(function(){
 		  upravitOdkazy($(this));
 		});
 	});
      </script>
